or whole if shorter\n    max_n=int(sr_ds*2.0)\n    y=sig_ds[:max_n] if len(sig_ds)>max_n else sig_ds\n    if len(y)<256:\n        flat=1.0\n        band_ratio=0.0\n        hiss_ratio=0.0\n    else:\n        # apply hann window\n        win=np.hanning(len(y))\n        Y=np.fft.rfft(y*win)\n        mag=np.abs(Y)+1e-12\n        # spectral flatness = geometric_mean/arithmetic_mean\n        flat=float(np.exp(np.mean(np.log(mag))) / (np.mean(mag)+1e-12))\n        freqs=np.fft.rfftfreq(len(y), 1/sr_ds)\n        # speech band 300-3400\n        speech_band=(freqs>=300)&(freqs<=3400)\n        total=np.sum(mag)\n        band=np.sum(mag[speech_band])\n        band_ratio=float(band/(total+1e-12))\n        # hiss band >6000\n        hiss=(freqs>=6000)&(freqs<=sr_ds/2)\n        hiss_ratio=float(np.sum(mag[hiss])/(total+1e-12))\n    return {\n        \"rms_db\": float(rms_db),\n        \"peak_db\": float(peak_db),\n        \"clip_ratio\": clip_ratio,\n        \"dc\": dc,\n        \"flatness\": flat,\n        \"band_ratio\": band_ratio,\n        \"hiss_ratio\": hiss_ratio,\n    }\n\n# compute for each merged segment\nseg_data=[]\nfor idx,(s,e) in enumerate(merged):\n    sig=x[s:e]\n    feat=segment_features(sig, sr)\n    feat[\"idx\"]=idx\n    feat[\"start_s\"]=s/sr\n    feat[\"end_s\"]=e/sr\n    feat[\"dur\"]= (e-s)/sr\n    seg_data.append(feat)\n\nseg_data[:2], len(seg_data)\n",

          "response_format_name": null,
          "text": "def segment_features(sig, sr):\n    rms=np.sqrt(np.mean(sig**2)+1e-12)\n    rms_db=20*np.log10(rms+1e-12)\n    peak=np.max(np.abs(sig))+1e-12\n    peak_db=20*np.log10(peak)\n    clip_ratio=float(np.mean(np.abs(sig)>0.98))\n    dc=float(np.mean(sig))\n    # downsample to 16000 for spectral stats\n    target_sr=16000\n    if sr==target_sr:\n        sig_ds=sig\n        sr_ds=sr\n    else:\n        if sr%target_sr==0:\n            factor=sr//target_sr\n            sig_ds=sig[::factor]\n            sr_ds=target_sr\n        else:\n            # linear resample\n            n_out=int(len(sig)*target_sr/sr)\n            t_in=np.linspace(0,1,len(sig),endpoint=False)\n            t_out=np.linspace(0,1,n_out,endpoint=False)\n            sig_ds=np.interp(t_out, t_in, sig).astype(np.float32)\n            sr_ds=target_sr\n    max_n=int(sr_ds*2.0)\n    y=sig_ds[:max_n] if len(sig_ds)>max_n else sig_ds\n    if len(y)<256:\n        flat=1.0\n        band_ratio=0.0\n        hiss_ratio=0.0\n    else:\n        win=np.hanning(len(y))\n        Y=np.fft.rfft(y*win)\n        mag=np.abs(Y)+1e-12\n        flat=float(np.exp(np.mean(np.log(mag))) / (np.mean(mag)+1e-12))\n        freqs=np.fft.rfftfreq(len(y), 1/sr_ds)\n        total=np.sum(mag)\n        band=np.sum(mag[(freqs>=300)&(freqs<=3400)])\n        band_ratio=float(band/(total+1e-12))\n        hiss=np.sum(mag[(freqs>=6000)&(freqs<=sr_ds/2)])\n        hiss_ratio=float(hiss/(total+1e-12))\n    return dict(rms_db=float(rms_db), peak_db=float(peak_db), clip_ratio=clip_ratio, dc=dc,\n                flatness=flat, band_ratio=band_ratio, hiss_ratio=hiss_ratio)\n\nphrase_data2=[]\nfor idx,(s,e) in enumerate(phrase_segs2):\n    sig=x[s:e]\n    feat=segment_features(sig, sr)\n    snr=feat[\"rms_db\"]-noise_floor\n    score=snr + 10*feat[\"band_ratio\"] - 20*feat[\"hiss_ratio\"] - 5*feat[\"flatness\"] - 200*feat[\"clip_ratio\"]\n    phrase_data2.append({\n        \"seg_idx\": idx, \"start\": s, \"end\": e, \"dur\": (e-s)/sr, \"score\": float(score),\n        \"start_s\": s/sr, \"end_s\": e/sr, \"snr_db\": float(snr), **feat\n    })\n\n# inspect score distribution\nscores=[d[\"score\"] for d in phrase_data2]\nnp.percentile(scores,[0,10,25,50,75,90,100]), len(scores)\n"

          "text": "import numpy as np, math\n\ndef segment_features(sig, sr):\n    # sig: float -1..1\n    # RMS dB\n    rms=np.sqrt(np.mean(sig**2)+1e-12)\n    rms_db=20*np.log10(rms+1e-12)\n    peak=np.max(np.abs(sig))+1e-12\n    peak_db=20*np.log10(peak)\n    clip_ratio=float(np.mean(np.abs(sig)>0.98))\n    # DC offset\n    dc=float(np.mean(sig))\n    # spectral flatness & band ratios\n    # downsample to 16000 for analysis\n    target_sr=16000\n    if sr!=target_sr:\n        # simple decimate via slicing using rational factor if divisible\n        factor=sr//target_sr\n        if sr%target_sr==0:\n            sig_ds=sig[::factor]\n            sr_ds=target_sr\n        else:\n            # fallback: linear interpolation\n            idx=np.arange(0,len(sig))*target_sr/sr\n            idx2=np.arange(int(len(sig)*target_sr/sr))\n            sig_ds=np.interp(idx2, idx, sig).astype(np.float32)\n            sr_ds=target_sr\n    else:\n        sig_ds=sig\n        sr_ds=sr\n    # take up to first 2 seconds for spectral stats; or whole if shorter\n    max_n=int(sr_ds*2.0)\n    y=sig_ds[:max_n] if len(sig_ds)>max_n else sig_ds\n    if len(y)<256:\n        flat=1.0\n        band_ratio=0.0\n        hiss_ratio=0.0\n    else:\n        # apply hann window\n        win=np.hanning(len(y))\n        Y=np.fft.rfft(y*win)\n        mag=np.abs(Y)+1e-12\n        # spectral flatness = geometric_mean/arithmetic_mean\n        flat=float(np.exp(np.mean(np.log(mag))) / (np.mean(mag)+1e-12))\n        freqs=np.fft.rfftfreq(len(y), 1/sr_ds)\n        # speech band 300-3400\n        speech_band=(freqs>=300)&(freqs<=3400)\n        total=np.sum(mag)\n        band=np.sum(mag[speech_band])\n        band_ratio=float(band/(total+1e-12))\n        # hiss band >6000\n        hiss=(freqs>=6000)&(freqs<=sr_ds/2)\n        hiss_ratio=float(np.sum(mag[hiss])/(total+1e-12))\n    return {\n        \"rms_db\": float(rms_db),\n        \"peak_db\": float(peak_db),\n        \"clip_ratio\": clip_ratio,\n        \"dc\": dc,\n        \"flatness\": flat,\n        \"band_ratio\": band_ratio,\n        \"hiss_ratio\": hiss_ratio,\n    }\n\n# compute for each merged segment\nseg_data=[]\nfor idx,(s,e) in enumerate(merged):\n    sig=x[s:e]\n    feat=segment_features(sig, sr)\n    feat[\"idx\"]=idx\n    feat[\"start_s\"]=s/sr\n    feat[\"end_s\"]=e/sr\n    feat[\"dur\"]= (e-s)/sr\n    seg_data.append(feat)\n\nseg_data[:2], len(seg_data)\n"
